*Do you like porn? Hate porn? Scared of the technology and the future?*

Whether you hate porn, love porn, or don't think feminist porn can exist,
if you're open to hearing more about the intersections of feminism and how
technology changing sex entertainment culture come to:

*#SellingSexy*


=E2=80=8B
=E2=80=8B
RSVP <https://www.facebook.com/events/402834866532240/>

A talk with Jincey Lumpkin, esq exploring how our social culture is
changing the future of entertainment. Lumpkin is a BGLTQ activist,
feminist, writer, and founder and executive of her company Juicy Pink Box.
She writes frequently about sex and feminism in her Huffington Post column,
and her company is dedicated to producing quality, feminist, sexy
pornography. Her talk will focus on a variety of issues surrounding
consent, consumerism and technology. If nothing else come to meet an
amazing queer woman!


=E2=80=8B


Cosponsored by the Radcliffe Union of Students

 Finale deserts will be served and delicious!


Part of Sex Week at Harvard College:
=E2=80=8BCheck out the schedule! <http://www.hsexweek.org/schedule/>
